<main id="site-content" role="main">

	<p>&nbsp;</p><h1 class="site-logo"><a href="http://pearson-eng.covid19-updates.co.uk/" class="custom-logo-link" rel="home"><img width="300" height="46" style="height: 46px;" src="http://pearson-eng.covid19-updates.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/sites/7/2020/03/pearsons-logo-600x93-1.jpg" class="custom-logo" alt="Pearson Engineering Covid-19 Updates" srcset="http://pearson-eng.covid19-updates.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/sites/7/2020/03/pearsons-logo-600x93-1.jpg 600w, http://pearson-eng.covid19-updates.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/sites/7/2020/03/pearsons-logo-600x93-1-300x47.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></a><span class="screen-reader-text">Pearson Engineering Covid-19 Updates</span></h1><p>&nbsp;</p><div class="section-inner medium text-center"><!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Pearson Engineering are continuing to communicate with both customers and suppliers.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>This portal has been designed specifically&nbsp;for staff so we can communicate coherently to all of our team what decisions are being&nbsp;made within the business surrounding the COV1D-19 outbreak. In addition to this so that you are kept well informed with&nbsp;<strong>official&nbsp;advice</strong>&nbsp;we have also linked the feed to update with Government&nbsp;updates every&nbsp;5 minutes.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Please keep checking in here for both Company &amp; Official Government updates.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>It is important that we all work together and act responsibly. As a business we are doing as much as we can to stop the spread of this outbreak and we ask our staff to try and make smart choices in order to protect themselves.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Uncertain times also bring opportunities so whilst it may seem like ‘doom and gloom’, this crisis will pass. As a business are in an extremely strong position and are structured in a way that will allow us to come through this in a positive manner.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph --></div><p>&nbsp;</p><div class="section-inner medium"><div class="responsive-tabs">

	<article class="post-55 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-guidance" id="post-">
					
						<header class="entry-header has-text-align-center">
							<div class="entry-header-inner section-inner medium">
								<div class="entry-categories">
									<span class="screen-reader-text">Categories</span>

										Guidance									</div><!-- .entry-categories-inner -->
								</div><!-- .entry-categories -->
								
								<h2 class="entry-title heading-size-1"><a target="_blank" href="https://www.gov.uk/government/publications/covid-19-residential-care-supported-living-and-home-care-guidance">Guidance: Coronavirus (COVID-19): residential care, supported living and home care guidance</a></h2>
		<div class="post-meta-wrapper post-meta-single post-meta-single-top">

			<ul class="post-meta">

									<li class="post-date meta-wrapper">
